<s> silenus i know not we will help you all we can <\s>
<s> 125 ulysses provide us food of which we are in want <\s>
<s> silenus here is not anything as i said but meat <\s>
<s> ulysses but meat is a sweet remedy for hunger <\s>

<s> 130 silenus but how much gold will you engage to give <\s>
<s> ulysses i bring no gold but bacchic juice <\s>
<s> tis long since these dry lips were wet with wine <\s>
<s> ulysses maron the son of the god gave it me <\s>
<s> silenus whom i have nursed a baby in my arms <\s>
<s> 135 ulysses the son of bacchus for your clearer knowledge <\s>
<s> silenus have you it now or is it in the ship <\s>
<s> ulysses old man this skin contains it which you see <\s>
<s> silenus why this would hardly be a mouthful for me <\s>
<s> ulysses nay twice as much as you can draw from thence <\s>

<s> ulysses would you first taste of the unmingled wine <\s>
<s> silenus tis just tasting invites the purchaser <\s>

<s> silenus pour that the draught may fillip my remembrance <\s>

<s> 200 outlaws or thieves <\s>

<s> 205 i have been beaten till i burn with fever <\s>
<s> who laid his fist upon your head <\s>
<s> silenus those men because i would not suffer them to steal your goods <\s>
<s> cyclops did not the rascals know i am a god sprung from the race of heaven <\s>
<s> 210 silenus i told them so but they bore off your things and ate the cheese in spite of all i said and carried out the lambs and said moreover they'd pin you down with a three cubit collar and pull your vitals out through your one eye 215 furrow your back with stripes then binding you throw you as ballast into the ship's hold and then deliver you a slave to move enormous rocks or found a vestibule <\s>

<s> nay haste and place in order quickly the cooking knives and heap upon the hearth 221 and kindle it a great faggot of wood as soon as they are slaughtered they shall fill my belly broiling warm from the live coals or boiled and seethed within the bubbling caldron <\s>
<s> 225 i am quite sick of the wild mountain game of stags and lions i have gorged enough and i grow hungry for the flesh of men <\s>

<s> may you perish wretch ulysses if i speak false <\s>

<s> silenus i know not we will help you all we can <\s>
<s> 125 ulysses provide us food of which we are in want <\s>
<s> silenus here is not anything as i said but meat <\s>
<s> ulysses but meat is a sweet remedy for hunger <\s>

<s> 130 silenus but how much gold will you engage to give <\s>
<s> ulysses i bring no gold but bacchic juice <\s>
<s> tis long since these dry lips were wet with wine <\s>
<s> ulysses maron the son of the god gave it me <\s>
<s> silenus whom i have nursed a baby in my arms <\s>
<s> 135 ulysses the son of bacchus for your clearer knowledge <\s>
<s> silenus have you it now or is it in the ship <\s>
<s> ulysses old man this skin contains it which you see <\s>
<s> silenus why this would hardly be a mouthful for me <\s>
<s> ulysses nay twice as much as you can draw from thence <\s>

<s> ulysses would you first taste of the unmingled wine <\s>
<s> silenus tis just tasting invites the purchaser <\s>

<s> silenus pour that the draught may fillip my remembrance <\s>

<s> 200 outlaws or thieves <\s>

<s> 205 i have been beaten till i burn with fever <\s>
<s> who laid his fist upon your head <\s>
<s> silenus those men because i would not suffer them to steal your goods <\s>
<s> cyclops did not the rascals know i am a god sprung from the race of heaven <\s>
<s> 210 silenus i told them so but they bore off your things and ate the cheese in spite of all i said and carried out the lambs and said moreover they'd pin you down with a three cubit collar and pull your vitals out through your one eye 215 furrow your back with stripes then binding you throw you as ballast into the ship's hold and then deliver you a slave to move enormous rocks or found a vestibule <\s>

<s> nay haste and place in order quickly the cooking knives and heap upon the hearth 221 and kindle it a great faggot of wood as soon as they are slaughtered they shall fill my belly broiling warm from the live coals or boiled and seethed within the bubbling caldron <\s>
<s> 225 i am quite sick of the wild mountain game of stags and lions i have gorged enough and i grow hungry for the flesh of men <\s>

<s> may you perish wretch ulysses if i speak false <\s>
